## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x0073 [0x32] ExtData[1]->MainSpeed = 13* * 0.1
  1: 0x0076 [0x1F] MOVE_ENTITY: EventEntity moves to X=-52.789*, Z=44.168*, Y=-0.199*
  2: 0x007E [0x1F] MOVE_ENTITY: Update entity position (mode=1)
  3: 0x0080 [0x00] END_REQSTACK()
```
